<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Biathlon World Championships</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>

<p>The first <b><a href="/wiki/Biathlon" title="Biathlon">Biathlon</a> World Championships</b> (<b>BWCH</b>) was held in 1958, with individual and team contests for men. The number of events has grown significantly over the years. Beginning in 1984, women biathletes had their own World Championships, and finally, from 1989, both genders have been participating in joint BWCHs. In 1978 the development was enhanced by the change from the large army rifle calibre to a small bore rifle, while the range to the target was reduced from 150 to 50 meters.</p>
<p></p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="BWCH_venues">BWCH venues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: BWCH venues">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The season's BWCHs takes place during February or March. Some years it has been necessary to schedule parts of the Championships at other than the main venue because of weather and/or snow conditions. Full, joint BWCHs have never been held in <a href="/wiki/Winter_Olympic_Games" title="Winter Olympic Games">Olympic Winter Games</a> seasons. BWCHs in non-IOC events, however, have been held in Olympic seasons. In 2005, the then new event of Mixed Relay (two legs done by women, two legs by men) was arranged separately from the ordinary Championships.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mass_start_.2815_km.29">Mass start (15 km)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Mass start (15 km)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event was first held in 1999.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Relay_.284_.C3.97_7.5_km.29">Relay (4 × 7.5 km)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Relay (4 × 7.5 km)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event was first held unofficially in <a href="/wiki/Biathlon_World_Championships_1965" title="Biathlon World Championships 1965">1965</a>. It was a success, and replaced the team competition as an official event in 1966.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Team_.28time.29">Team (time)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Team (time)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event was held from 1958 to 1965. The times of the top 3 athletes from each country in the 20 km individual were added together (in 1958 the top 4).</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Team">Team</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Team">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event, a patrol race, was held from 1989 to 1998. 1989-93: 20 km. 1994-98: 10 km.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Women">Women</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Women">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Individual_.2815_km.29">Individual (15 km)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Individual (15 km)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event was first held in 1984. Through 1988 the distance was 10 km.</p>

</tr>
</table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sprint_.287.5_km.29">Sprint (7.5 km)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Sprint (7.5 km)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event was first held in 1984. Through 1988 the distance was 5 km.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Relay_.284_.C3.97_6_km.29">Relay (4 × 6 km)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Relay (4 × 6 km)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event was first held in 1984. Through 1988, the event was 3 × 5 km. 1989-91: 3 × 7.5 km. 1993-2001: 4 × 7.5 km. In 2003, the leg distance was set to 6 km.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Team_2">Team</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Team">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event, a patrol race, was held from 1989 to 1998. 1989-93: 15 km. 1994-98: 7.5 km.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Mixed">Mixed</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Mixed">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Relay_.282_.C3.97_6_km_.2B_2_.C3.97_7.5_km.29">Relay (2 × 6 km + 2 × 7.5 km)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Biathlon_World_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Relay (2 × 6 km + 2 × 7.5 km)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>This event was first held in 2005, at the <a href="/wiki/Biathlon_World_Cup" title="Biathlon World Cup">Biathlon World Cup</a> finals in <a href="/wiki/Khanty-Mansiysk" title="Khanty-Mansiysk">Khanty-Mansiysk</a>. In 2005 the women biathletes did the first two legs, and the men did the following two, while in 2006 the sequence was woman–man–woman–man. At the <a href="/wiki/Biathlon_World_Championships_2007" title="Biathlon World Championships 2007">Biathlon World Championships 2007</a> in <a href="/wiki/Rasen-Antholz" title="Rasen-Antholz">Antholz</a>, the sequence was women–women–man–man. The men ski legs of 7.5 km (in 2005-06: 6 km) and the women ski 6 km each. From 2007 only one team per nation is allowed to compete.</p>
